Little Easter egg story:
Shenzhen-Shanwei Cooperation Zone is China's first special cooperation zone. It belongs to Haifeng County, Shanwei City, Guangdong Province. It is a cooperative project between Shenzhen and Shanwei. My personal understanding is that Shenzhen lacks land for development, and an area (mountainous rural area) has been allocated to Shenzhen in Haifeng, which will be managed and developed by the Shenzhen government. All local residents will be transferred to Shenzhen household registration, which can be regarded as a blessing from heaven [naughty]
